The Gazette of the Democratic Socialist Republic of  Sri Lanka 
PART III - LANDS 
 
FINAL ORDERS 
 
LAND SETTLEMENT ORDINANCE 
 
Settlement Orders No. 450 (Badulla) 
 
Whereas a settlement notice under Section 4 of the Land Settlement Ordinance was duly published in the  Gazette No. 79 of 28th Sep-
tember 1973 and as otherwise required by the said S ection, in respect of the lands situated in the vil lage of Main area in Binthenna 
Korale Binthenna (Then Mahiyanganaya) Divisional Re venue officer‚Äôs Division ( Now Mahiyanganaya Divisi onal Secretary‚Äôs Divi-
sion) of the Badulla District in the Uva Province and Described as Lot no. 01 in Block Survey Topo Plan No. 57(Uva) (Vide Settlement 
Notice No. 4470 (Badulla)).  
 
And whereas all claims received  in pursuance of the said notice have been duly dealt with in  accordance with the provisions of the said 
Ordinance: 
 
I, the undersigned, in pursuance of the powers conf erred on me by Section 5(5) of the said Ordinance d o hereby make order that the 
lands or portions thereof be settled as specified in the Schedule to this order.  
 
  P.M.H.P
RIYADHARSHANI, 
  Assistant Settlement Officer 
  Commissioner of - 
  Land Title Settlement. 
  
Given at 
Land Title Settlement Department, 
Battaramulla this 
05th February, 2016. 
N.B.‚Äì This Extraordinary Gazette can be downloaded from www.documents.gov.lk
